',  ', See more', Like',   ', Comment',   ', Share', Mayank Dugar', 13 December 2016 at 09:41', Dear MUN Enthusiasts,
It is a moment of extreme joy to welcome you t', ...', o the 1st edition of Jain International Residential School Model United Nations.
Model United Nations is an exemplary educational platform available for the next generation of world leaders to enrich their thought-process and shape their character. It lays down a path to attain the much-neededdiplomacy and wit to develop into a successful citizen of the 21st century. 
MUN\u2019s imbibe in student\u2019s imperative skills of society such as communication and interaction. Oratory and debating skills come hand in hand with the intense 3 day MUNning experience. It often leaves behind a zeal in all MUNers to keep the torch of learning alight.
JIRS Model United Nations Society this year aims to deliver to you 3 intense days of ardent debate and inspiring Committee Agendas which are of great significance to the global citizen 
JIRSMUN Conference 2017 will be a simulation of eight Committees: 
United Nations Security Council(UNSC), 
United Nations Human Rights Council(UNHRC), 
Disarmament and International Security Council (DISEC),
Economic and Social Council (ECOSOC),
United Nations Environmental Programme (UNEP),
United Nations Cyber Security Task Force (UNCSTF),
Indo\u2013Pak Meet 
Isis Crisis Committee
JIRS is a pioneer in the field of education that focuses on the holistic development of a child. Its ranked 1st in the country by the famous Educational World on vital parameters of infrastructure, sports, pastoral care, health and hygiene. JIRS is one among the top 14 schools in India to secure highest rating of 5 stars by The Pioneer among all categories of schools. The only school from Bangalore, from the state of Karnataka and one among the two fully residential schools in South India to achieve the laurels.

JIRSMUN 2017 is an extraordinary intellectual and social conference that brings together an absolutely amazing assortment of young minds from across India to engage in cultural exchange and gain first-hand experience of negotiating processes by playing the role of diplomats. They unfailingly leave a priceless page in the book of memories of all those associated with it.
JIRSMUN 2017 will provide students & young professionals with the opportunity to improve their knowledge and awareness of the most relevant international issues and contribute to advanced, feasible and innovative proposals for action.
On this note The Organizing Committee,extends a hearty welcome to you and looks forward for being your host at the 1st Jain International Model United Nations Conference, 2017.

For more details, join us on JIRS MUN FB Page or ', jirsmun.com', 

Yours Truly,

',  ', See more', Like',   ', Comment',   ', Share', Mayank Dugar', 13 December 2016 at 09:41', Dear MUN Enthusiasts,
It is a moment of extreme joy to welcome you t', ...', o the 1st edition of Jain International Residential School Model United Nations.
Model United Nations is an exemplary educational platform available for the next generation of world leaders to enrich their thought-process and shape their character. It lays down a path to attain the much-neededdiplomacy and wit to develop into a successful citizen of the 21st century. 
MUN\u2019s imbibe in student\u2019s imperative skills of society such as communication and interaction. Oratory and debating skills come hand in hand with the intense 3 day MUNning experience. It often leaves behind a zeal in all MUNers to keep the torch of learning alight.
JIRS Model United Nations Society this year aims to deliver to you 3 intense days of ardent debate and inspiring Committee Agendas which are of great significance to the global citizen 
JIRSMUN Conference 2017 will be a simulation of eight Committees: 
United Nations Security Council(UNSC), 
United Nations Human Rights Council(UNHRC), 
Disarmament and International Security Council (DISEC),
Economic and Social Council (ECOSOC),
United Nations Environmental Programme (UNEP),
United Nations Cyber Security Task Force (UNCSTF),
Indo\u2013Pak Meet 
Isis Crisis Committee
JIRS is a pioneer in the field of education that focuses on the holistic development of a child. Its ranked 1st in the country by the famous Educational World on vital parameters of infrastructure, sports, pastoral care, health and hygiene. JIRS is one among the top 14 schools in India to secure highest rating of 5 stars by The Pioneer among all categories of schools. The only school from Bangalore, from the state of Karnataka and one among the two fully residential schools in South India to achieve the laurels.

JIRSMUN 2017 is an extraordinary intellectual and social conference that brings together an absolutely amazing assortment of young minds from across India to engage in cultural exchange and gain first-hand experience of negotiating processes by playing the role of diplomats. They unfailingly leave a priceless page in the book of memories of all those associated with it.
JIRSMUN 2017 will provide students & young professionals with the opportunity to improve their knowledge and awareness of the most relevant international issues and contribute to advanced, feasible and innovative proposals for action.
On this note The Organizing Committee,extends a hearty welcome to you and looks forward for being your host at the 1st Jain International Model United Nations Conference, 2017.

For more details, join us on JIRS MUN FB Page or ', jirsmun.com', 

Yours Truly,
